Our team, products, and process will continuously evolve. It&#x27;s on each of us to be future-forward in our approach and strategically pivot as one. It&#x27;s how we&#x27;ll grow thoughtfully and stay parent-centric. It’s how we’ll keep changing everything for the better.</p></div></div></div><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItem" class><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemHeading" aria-level="3" role="heading" class="accordion__heading"><div class="accordion__button" id="accordion__heading-:R5576:" aria-disabled="false" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="accordion__panel-:R5576:" role="button" tabindex="0" data-accordion-component="AccordionItemButton"><h2 class="valuesList_value__oW6oz h-38 lg:h-80 black1">Engineer the better.</h2></div></div><div hidden class="accordion__panel-wrapper"><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemPanel" class="accordion__panel" id="accordion__panel-:R5576:"><p class="p-14 lg:p-17 black7 valuesList_text__aLm_x">We are diaper engineers, all of us. Steeped in scientific discovery, none of this is by chance. Each day, we are designing wins. We are developing new answers. We are innovating and challenging what’s been accepted, and what’s been done. We are thoughtfully engineering better solutions, even when society says it’s solved.</p></div></div></div><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItem" class><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemHeading" aria-level="3" role="heading" class="accordion__heading"><div class="accordion__button" id="accordion__heading-:R7576:" aria-disabled="false" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="accordion__panel-:R7576:" role="button" tabindex="0" data-accordion-component="AccordionItemButton"><h2 class="valuesList_value__oW6oz h-38 lg:h-80 black1">Stay curious.</h2></div></div><div hidden class="accordion__panel-wrapper"><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemPanel" class="accordion__panel" id="accordion__panel-:R7576:"><p class="p-14 lg:p-17 black7 valuesList_text__aLm_x">This is our space to explore, question, test and learn. As we reimagine baby care solutions, we defy expectations and alter the status quo. That takes guts. It’s why we keep asking what others wouldn’t dare to dream.</p></div></div></div><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItem" class><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemHeading" aria-level="3" role="heading" class="accordion__heading"><div class="accordion__button" id="accordion__heading-:R9576:" aria-disabled="false" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="accordion__panel-:R9576:" role="button" tabindex="0" data-accordion-component="AccordionItemButton"><h2 class="valuesList_value__oW6oz h-38 lg:h-80 black1">Highlight performance.</h2></div></div><div hidden class="accordion__panel-wrapper"><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemPanel" class="accordion__panel" id="accordion__panel-:R9576:"><p class="p-14 lg:p-17 black7 valuesList_text__aLm_x">We have the highest performing products, and the highest performing people. Everyone can make an impact. We motivate and root for each other. We shine the spotlight on others, and share our appreciation for exceptional work. As a company, we take pride in how we care for and support our team.</p></div></div></div><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItem" class><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemHeading" aria-level="3" role="heading" class="accordion__heading"><div class="accordion__button" id="accordion__heading-:Rb576:" aria-disabled="false" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="accordion__panel-:Rb576:" role="button" tabindex="0" data-accordion-component="AccordionItemButton"><h2 class="valuesList_value__oW6oz h-38 lg:h-80 black1">Even simpler.</h2></div></div><div hidden class="accordion__panel-wrapper"><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemPanel" class="accordion__panel" id="accordion__panel-:Rb576:"><p class="p-14 lg:p-17 black7 valuesList_text__aLm_x">We know what’s important. And what is not. Within each of us is a quest to extract the simplest, truest form. We prefer less and better. Quality over quantity. And concise communication. Simple? How about, even simpler.</p></div></div></div><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItem" class><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemHeading" aria-level="3" role="heading" class="accordion__heading"><div class="accordion__button" id="accordion__heading-:Rd576:" aria-disabled="false" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="accordion__panel-:Rd576:" role="button" tabindex="0" data-accordion-component="AccordionItemButton"><h2 class="valuesList_value__oW6oz h-38 lg:h-80 black1">Free of egos.</h2></div></div><div hidden class="accordion__panel-wrapper"><div data-accordion-component="AccordionItemPanel" class="accordion__panel" id="accordion__panel-:Rd576:"><p class="p-14 lg:p-17 black7 valuesList_text__aLm_x">Just the way we are free of harsh chemicals, parabens, phthalates, and fragrances — we are free of egos, too. This is a place of compassion, collaboration, and high integrity. A space for comradery and kindness. There’s no room for self-serving intentions here. No toxins welcome.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></section></div><div data-type="titleTextCtaFigure"><figure role="none" class="titleTextCtaFigure_figure__rx56j lg:screen-h"
